## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

## Core Signature Implementation Files

1. **`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`** - The main signature calculation file. Contains:
   - `PluginManifest` struct (manifest data structure)
   - `Signature` struct (implements `SignatureCalculator`)
   - `Calculate()` - main signature calculation
   - `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()` - reads MANIFEST.txt
   - `readPluginManifest()` - parses and verifies manifest
   - `validateManifest()` - validates manifest fields
   - `Verify()` - PGP signature verification using OpenPGP
   - `verifyHash()` - SHA256 file hash verification
   - `urlMatch()` - root URL matching

2. **`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`** - Signature validation on load. Contains:
   - `Validator` interface
   - `Validation` struct
   - `ValidateSignature()` - validates plugin signature status on load
   - `ProvideValidatorService()` / `NewValidator()`

3. **`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`** - Unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement. Contains:
   - `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct
   - `CanLoadPlugin()` - checks if unsigned plugin is allowed (via allowlist or dev mode)
   - `ProvideOSSAuthorizer()` / `NewUnsignedAuthorizer()`

4. **`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`** - Static (hardcoded) public key. Contains:
   - `KeyRetriever` struct
   - `GetPublicKey()` - returns hardcoded Grafana public key
   - `GetDefaultKey()` / `GetDefaultKeyID()`

## Key Store / Key Retrieval Files

5. **`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`** - Key retriever service that selects between static and dynamic. Contains:
   - `Service` struct

The answer.json has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Plugin Signature Verification in Grafana

I identified **23 Go source files** across the codebase that implement plugin signature verification:

### Core Signature Files (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/`)
- **`manifest.go`** — The heart of the system: reads `MANIFEST.txt`, decodes PGP clearsign blocks, validates manifest fields, verifies PGP signatures via OpenPGP, and checks SHA-256 hashes of all plugin files
- **`signature.go`** — Load-time validation: checks computed signature status and enforces allow/reject decisions (with parent plugin signature inheritance)
- **`authorizer.go`** — Unsigned plugin allowlist: `CanLoadPlugin()` permits unsigned plugins only in dev mode or if the plugin ID is in `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins`
- **`statickey/static_retriever.go`** — Hardcoded Grafana PGP public key (key ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`)

### Public Key Management
- **`keyretriever/retriever.go`** — Selects static vs. dynamic key retrieval
- **`keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`** — Downloads/caches keys from grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys`), refreshed every 10 days
- **`keystore/keystore.go`** — KV-backed public key store

### Pipeline Integration
- **`pipeline/validation/steps.go`** — `PluginSignatureValidator` as a validation pipeline step
- **`pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`** — `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` calls `Calculate()` during bootstrap
- **`services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`** — Integration-layer `SignatureValidation`

### Configuration & Interfaces
- **`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`** — `SignatureCalculator`, `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`, `KeyStore`, `KeyRetriever` interfaces
- **`pkg/plugins/models.go`** — `SignatureStatus` and `SignatureType` types

**Manifest signing & verification** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`):
- Reads `MANIFEST.txt` (PGP clearsign format)
- Verifies PGP signature using OpenPGP with Grafana's public key
- Validates SHA-256 hashes of all plugin files
- Checks root URL matching for private plugins

**Signature validation on load** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`):
- `ValidateSignature()` enforces allow/reject based on computed status
- Handles parent→child signature inheritance for nested plugins

**Unsigned plugin allowlist** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`):
- `CanLoadPlugin()` checks `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` config list and dev mode flag

**Public key management**:
- Static hardcoded key (`statickey/static_retriever.go`)
- Dynamic key download from grafana.com API (`keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`)
- KV-backed key store (`keystore/keystore.go`)

**Pipeline integration**: Bootstrap stage computes signatures; validation stage enforces them.

**Configuration**: `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` flows from `grafana.ini` → `setting_plugins.go` → `pluginconfig/config.go` → `PluginManagementCfg` → `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`.
